/****** Object:  View [dbo].[vUnbalancedJournalEntries]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:52 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[vUnbalancedJournalEntries] AS
SELECT je.Id AS JournalEntryId,
       SUM(jed.Debit) AS TotalDebit,
       SUM(jed.Credit) AS TotalCredit
FROM dbo.JournalEntry je
JOIN dbo.JournalEntryDetail jed ON je.Id = jed.JournalEntryId
GROUP BY je.Id
HAVING SUM(jed.Debit) <> SUM(jed.Credit);
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[SalesOrderHeader](
	[Id] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[CompanyCustomerId] [int] NOT NULL,
	[AddressId] [int] NOT NULL,
	[SalesChannelId] [int] NOT NULL,
	[SalesOrderId]  AS (case when [SalesChannelId]=(2) OR [Confirmed]=(1) then 'SO'+right('00000000'+CONVERT([varchar](8),[Id]),(8))  end) PERSISTED,
	[OnlineOrderId]  AS (case when [SalesChannelId]=(1) then 'ON'+right('00000000'+CONVERT([varchar](8),[Id]),(8))  end) PERSISTED,
	[DirectOrderId]  AS (case when [SalesChannelId]=(2) then 'DO'+right('00000000'+CONVERT([varchar](8),[Id]),(8))  end) PERSISTED,
	[OrderDate] [datetime] NOT NULL,
	[TotalAmount] [decimal](18, 2) NOT NULL,
	[DiscountAmount] [decimal](18, 2) NOT NULL,
	[NetAmount]  AS ([TotalAmount]-[DiscountAmount]) PERSISTED,
	[SessionId] [nvarchar](100) NULL,
	[IPAddress] [varchar](45) NULL,
	[Status] [nvarchar](30) NOT NULL,
	[IsActive] [bit] NOT NULL,
	[Confirmed] [bit] NOT NULL,
	[CreatedBy] [nvarchar](100) NULL,
	[CreatedAt] [datetime] NOT NULL,
	[UpdatedBy] [nvarchar](100) NULL,
	[UpdatedAt] [datetime] NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK__SalesOrd__3214EC070A447194] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[Id] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON, OPTIMIZE_FOR_SEQUENTIAL_KEY = OFF) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]

GO

GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetAccountByQuery]
(
	@Query	nvarchar(4000)
)
AS
BEGIN 

SET @Query = isnull(@Query, '')
DECLARE @SQL1 nvarchar(4000)

IF (@Query != '')
BEGIN
	SET @Query = 'WHERE ' + char(13) + @Query	
END

SET @SQL1 =		'SELECT * 
				FROM 
				[dbo].[Account] ' + @Query
								
EXEC sp_executesql @SQL1

RETURN @@ROWCOUNT
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetAttributeNameByQuery]

	@Query	nvarchar(4000)
)
AS
BEGIN 

SET @Query = isnull(@Query, '')
DECLARE @SQL1 nvarchar(4000)

IF (@Query != '')
BEGIN
	SET @Query = 'WHERE ' + char(13) + @Query	
END

SET @SQL1 =		'SELECT * 
				FROM 
				[dbo].[AttributeName] ' + @Query
								
EXEC sp_executesql @SQL1

RETURN @@ROWCOUNT
END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetPagedAccount]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetPagedAccount]
(
	@TotalRows		int	OUTPUT,
	@PageIndex	int,
	@RowPerPage		int,
	@WhereClause	nvarchar(4000),
	@SortColumn		nvarchar(128),
	@SortOrder		nvarchar(4)
)
AS
BEGIN 

SET @PageIndex = isnull(@PageIndex, -1)
SET @RowPerPage = isnull(@RowPerPage, -1)
SET @WhereClause = isnull(@WhereClause, '')
SET @SortColumn = isnull(@SortColumn, '')
SET @SortOrder = isnull(@SortOrder, '')
SET @TotalRows = 0
SET @RowPerPage = @RowPerPage -1
DECLARE @SQL1 nvarchar(4000)
DECLARE @SQL2 nvarchar(4000)

IF (@WhereClause != '')
BEGIN
	SET @WhereClause = 'WHERE ' + char(13) + @WhereClause	
END

IF (@SortColumn != '')
BEGIN
	SET @SortColumn = 'ORDER BY ' + @SortColumn

	IF (@SortOrder != '')
	BEGIN
		SET @SortColumn = @SortColumn + ' ' + @SortOrder
	END
END
ELSE
BEGIN
	SET @SortColumn = @SortColumn + ' ORDER BY [Id] ASC'
END

SET @SQL1 = 'WITH AccountEntries AS (
			SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER ('+ @SortColumn +')AS Row,
	[Id],
	[AccountCode],
	[AccountName],
	[AccountTypeId],
	[IsActive],
	[Description],
	[Balance],
	[CurrencyCode],
	[ParentAccountId],
	[CreatedBy],
	[CreatedAt],
	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt]
				FROM 
				[dbo].[Account]
					'+ @WhereClause +'
				)
				SELECT 
	[Id],
	[AccountCode],
	[AccountName],
	[AccountTypeId],
	[IsActive],
	[Description],
	[Balance],
	[CurrencyCode],
	[ParentAccountId],
	[CreatedBy],
	[CreatedAt],
	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt]
				FROM 
					AccountEntries
				WHERE 
					Row between '+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) + 1) +'And ('+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) +@RowPerPage+ 1) +')'
	

SET @SQL2 =		' SELECT @TotalRows = COUNT(*) 
				FROM 
				[dbo].[Account] ' + @WhereClause
								
EXEC sp_executesql @SQL2, N'@TotalRows int output', @TotalRows = @TotalRows output

EXEC sp_executesql @SQL1

RETURN @@ROWCOUNT
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetPagedAccountType]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetPagedAccountType]
(
	@TotalRows		int	OUTPUT,
	@PageIndex	int,
	@RowPerPage		int,
	@WhereClause	nvarchar(4000),

BEGIN 

SET @PageIndex = isnull(@PageIndex, -1)

SET @SortColumn = isnull(@SortColumn, '')
SET @SortOrder = isnull(@SortOrder, '')
SET @TotalRows = 0

IF (@WhereClause != '')

IF (@SortColumn != '')

	BEGIN
		SET @SortColumn = @SortColumn + ' ' + @SortOrder
	END

ELSE
BEGIN

	[Name],
	[Description],
	[CreatedBy],
	[CreatedAt],
	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt]
				FROM 
				[dbo].[AccountType]
					'+ @WhereClause +'
				)

	[Id],
	[Name],
	[Description],
	[CreatedBy],
	[CreatedAt],
	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt]
				FROM 
					AccountTypeEntries
				WHERE 
					Row between '+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) + 1) +'And ('+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) +@RowPerPage+ 1) +')'
	

SET @SQL2 =		' SELECT @TotalRows = COUNT(*)

	[PoReceivedId],

	[InOut],
	[Date],
	[Price],
	[Quantity],
	[CreatedBy],
	[CreatedAt],
	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt],
	[Remarks]
				FROM 
					InventoryTransactionEntries
				WHERE 
					Row between '+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) + 1) +'And ('+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) +@RowPerPage+ 1) +')'
	

SET @SQL2 =		' SELECT @TotalRows = COUNT(*) 
				FROM 
				[dbo].[InventoryTransaction] ' + @WhereClause
								
EXEC sp_executesql @SQL2, N'@TotalRows int output', @TotalRows = @TotalRows output

EXEC sp_executesql @SQL1

RETURN @@ROWCOUNT
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetPagedJournalEntry]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetPagedJournalEntry]
(
	@TotalRows		int	OUTPUT,
	@PageIndex	int,
	@RowPerPage		int,
	@WhereClause	nvarchar(4000),
	@SortColumn		nvarchar(128),
	@SortOrder		nvarchar(4)
)
AS
BEGIN 

SET @PageIndex = isnull(@PageIndex, -1)
SET @RowPerPage = isnull(@RowPerPage, -1)
SET @WhereClause = isnull(@WhereClause, '')
SET @SortColumn = isnull(@SortColumn, '')
SET @SortOrder = isnull(@SortOrder, '')
SET @TotalRows = 0
SET @RowPerPage = @RowPerPage -1
DECLARE @SQL1 nvarchar(4000)
DECLARE @SQL2 nvarchar(4000)

IF (@WhereClause != '')
BEGIN
	SET @WhereClause = 'WHERE ' + char(13) + @WhereClause	
END

IF (@SortColumn != '')
BEGIN
	SET @SortColumn = 'ORDER BY ' + @SortColumn

	IF (@SortOrder != '')
	BEGIN
		SET @SortColumn = @SortColumn + ' ' + @SortOrder
	END
END
ELSE
BEGIN
	SET @SortColumn = @SortColumn + ' ORDER BY [Id] ASC'
END

SET @SQL1 = 'WITH JournalEntryEntries AS (
			SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER ('+ @SortColumn +')AS Row,
	[Id],
	[ReferenceType],
	[ReferenceId],
	[EntryDate],
	[Description],
	[CreatedBy],
	[CreatedAt],
	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt]
				FROM 
				[dbo].[JournalEntry]
					'+ @WhereClause +'
				)
				SELECT 
	[Id],
	[ReferenceType],
	[ReferenceId],
	[EntryDate],
	[Description],
	[CreatedBy],
	[CreatedAt],
	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt]
				FROM 
					JournalEntryEntries
				WHERE 
					Row between '+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) + 1) +'And ('+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) +@RowPerPage+ 1) +')'
	

SET @SQL2 =		' SELECT @TotalRows = COUNT(*) 
				FROM 
				[dbo].[JournalEntry] ' + @WhereClause
								
EXEC sp_executesql @SQL2, N'@TotalRows int output', @TotalRows = @TotalRows output

EXEC sp_executesql @SQL1

RETURN @@ROWCOUNT
END
GO

SET @RowPerPage = isnull(@RowPerPage, -1)
SET @WhereClause = isnull(@WhereClause, '')
SET @SortColumn = isnull(@SortColumn, '')
SET @SortOrder = isnull(@SortOrder, '')
SET @TotalRows = 0
SET @RowPerPage = @RowPerPage -1
DECLARE @SQL1 nvarchar(4000)
DECLARE @SQL2 nvarchar(4000)

IF (@WhereClause != '')
BEGIN
	SET @WhereClause = 'WHERE ' + char(13) + @WhereClause	
END

IF (@SortColumn != '')
BEGIN
	SET @SortColumn = 'ORDER BY ' + @SortColumn

	IF (@SortOrder != '')
	BEGIN
		SET @SortColumn = @SortColumn + ' ' + @SortOrder
	END
END
ELSE
BEGIN
	SET @SortColumn = @SortColumn + ' ORDER BY [Id] ASC'
END

SET @SQL1 = 'WITH PoRequestedEntries AS (
			SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER ('+ @SortColumn +')AS Row,
	[Id],
	[VendorId],
	[ProductId],
	[Quantity],
	[RequestDate],
	[Status],
	[CreatedBy],
	[CreatedAt],
	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt],
	[Remarks],
	[ReferenceNo]
				FROM 
				[dbo].[PoRequested]
					'+ @WhereClause +'
				)
				SELECT 
	[Id],
	[VendorId],
	[ProductId],
	[Quantity],
	[RequestDate],
	[Status],
	[CreatedBy],
	[CreatedAt],
	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt],
	[Remarks],
	[ReferenceNo]
				FROM 
					PoRequestedEntries
				WHERE 
					Row between '+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) + 1) +'And ('+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) +@RowPerPage+ 1) +')'
	

SET @SQL2 =		' SELECT @TotalRows = COUNT(*) 
				FROM 
				[dbo].[PoRequested] ' + @WhereClause
								
EXEC sp_executesql @SQL2, N'@TotalRows int output', @TotalRows = @TotalRows output

EXEC sp_executesql @SQL1

RETURN @@ROWCOUNT
END

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetPagedProduct]
(
	@TotalRows		int	OUTPUT,
	@PageIndex	int,
	@RowPerPage		int,
	@WhereClause	nvarchar(4000),
	@SortColumn		nvarchar(128),
	@SortOrder		nvarchar(4)
)
AS
BEGIN 

SET @PageIndex = isnull(@PageIndex, -1)
SET @RowPerPage = isnull(@RowPerPage, -1)

		SET @SortColumn = @SortColumn + ' ' + @SortOrder
	END
END
ELSE

	SET @SortColumn = @SortColumn + ' ORDER BY [Id] ASC'

	[IsActive],
	[CreatedBy],

	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt]

				WHERE 
					Row between '+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) + 1) +'And ('+ CONVERT(nvarchar(10), (@PageIndex * @RowPerPage) +@RowPerPage+ 1) +')'

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetPaymentAllocationMaximumId]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/

GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetPaymentAllocationMaximumId]
AS
	DECLARE @Result int
	SET @Result = 0
	
	SELECT @Result = MAX(Id) 		
	FROM
		[dbo].[PaymentAllocation]

	If @Result > 0 
		BEGIN
			-- Everything is OK
			RETURN @Result
		END
		ELSE
		BEGIN
			RETURN 0
		END
RETURN @Result
GO

	@Query	nvarchar(4000)
)
AS
BEGIN 

SET @Query = isnull(@Query, '')
DECLARE @SQL1 nvarchar(4000)

IF (@Query != '')
BEGIN
	SET @Query = 'WHERE ' + char(13) + @Query	
END

SET @SQL1 =		'SELECT * 
				FROM 
				[dbo].[PaymentMethod] ' + @Query
								
EXEC sp_executesql @SQL1

RETURN @@ROWCOUNT
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetPaymentMethodMaximumId]

	If @Result > 0 
		BEGIN
			-- Everything is OK
			RETURN @Result
		END
		ELSE
		BEGIN
			RETURN 0
		END
RETURN @Result
GO

	DECLARE @Result int
	SET @Result = 0
	
	SELECT @Result = MAX(Id) 		
	FROM
		[dbo].[ProductImage]

	If @Result > 0 
		BEGIN
			-- Everything is OK
			RETURN @Result
		END
		ELSE
		BEGIN
			RETURN 0
		END
RETURN @Result
GO

EXEC sp_executesql @SQL1

RETURN @@ROWCOUNT
END

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[InsertAccount]
(
	@Id int OUTPUT,
	@AccountCode nvarchar(20),
	@AccountName nvarchar(100),
	@AccountTypeId int,
	@IsActive bit,
	@Description nvarchar(255),
	@Balance decimal(18, 2),
	@CurrencyCode nvarchar(10),
	@ParentAccountId int,
	@CreatedBy nvarchar(100),
	@CreatedAt datetime,
	@UpdatedBy nvarchar(100),
	@UpdatedAt datetime
)
AS
    INSERT INTO [dbo].[Account] 
	(
	[AccountCode],
	[AccountName],
	[AccountTypeId],
	[IsActive],
	[Description],
	[Balance],
	[CurrencyCode],
	[ParentAccountId],
	[CreatedBy],
	[CreatedAt],
	[UpdatedBy],
	[UpdatedAt]
    ) 
	VALUES 
	(
	@AccountCode,
	@AccountName,
	@AccountTypeId,
	@IsActive,
	@Description,
	@Balance,
	@CurrencyCode,
	@ParentAccountId,
	@CreatedBy,
	@CreatedAt,
	@UpdatedBy,
	@UpdatedAt
    )
	DECLARE @Err int
	DECLARE @Result int

	SET @Result = @@ROWCOUNT
	SET @Err = @@ERROR 
	If @Err <> 0 
	BEGIN
		SET @Id = -1
		RETURN @Err
	END
	ELSE
	BEGIN
		If @Result = 1 
		BEGIN
			-- Everything is OK
			SET @Id = @@IDENTITY
		END
		ELSE
		BEGIN
			SET @Id = -1
			RETURN 0
		END
	END

	RETURN @Id
GO

	DECLARE @Result int

	BEGIN
		SET @Id = -1
		RETURN @Err
	END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_GetProductDetails]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetProductDetails]
    @ProductId INT
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- 1. Get Base Product
    SELECT * FROM [dbo].[Product] WHERE Id = @ProductId;

    -- 2. Get Base Product Images
    SELECT * FROM [dbo].[ProductImage] WHERE ProductId = @ProductId ORDER BY SortOrder;

    -- 3. Get Product Variants
    SELECT * FROM [dbo].[ProductVariant] WHERE ProductId = @ProductId AND IsActive = 1;

    -- Create a temp table of the variant IDs for faster lookups
    SELECT Id INTO #VariantIds FROM [dbo].[ProductVariant] WHERE ProductId = @ProductId AND IsActive = 1;

    -- 4. Get Variant Price/Stock (using the temp table)
    SELECT * FROM [dbo].[VariantPriceStock] WHERE Id IN (SELECT Id FROM #VariantIds);

    -- 5. Get Variant-Specific Images (using the temp table)
    SELECT * FROM [dbo].[VariantImage] WHERE VariantId IN (SELECT Id FROM #VariantIds) ORDER BY DisplayOrder;

    -- 6. Get Product Options (e.g., "Color", "Size")
    -- We join AttributeName to get the name
    SELECT
        pa.AttributeId,
        an.Name AS AttributeName
    FROM [dbo].[ProductAttribute] pa
    JOIN [dbo].[AttributeName] an ON pa.AttributeId = an.Id
    WHERE pa.ProductId = @ProductId
    ORDER BY pa.DisplayOrder;

    -- 7. Get All *Possible* Values for those options (e.g., "Silver", "Black", "512GB")
    SELECT
        av.*
    FROM [dbo].[AttributeValue] av
    WHERE av.AttributeId IN (SELECT AttributeId FROM [dbo].[ProductAttribute] WHERE ProductId = @ProductId)
    ORDER BY av.DisplayOrder;

    -- 8. Get the Variant-to-Value Mappings
    SELECT * FROM [dbo].[VariantAttributeValue] WHERE VariantId IN (SELECT Id FROM #VariantIds);

    -- Drop the temp table
    DROP TABLE #VariantIds;

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[UpdateAccount]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[UpdateAccount]
(
	@Id int,
	@AccountCode nvarchar(20),
	@AccountName nvarchar(100),
	@AccountTypeId int,
	@IsActive bit,
	@Description nvarchar(255),
	@Balance decimal(18, 2),
	@CurrencyCode nvarchar(10),
	@ParentAccountId int,
	@CreatedBy nvarchar(100),
	@CreatedAt datetime,
	@UpdatedBy nvarchar(100),
	@UpdatedAt datetime
)
AS
    UPDATE [dbo].[Account] 
	SET
	[AccountCode] = @AccountCode,
	[AccountName] = @AccountName,
	[AccountTypeId] = @AccountTypeId,
	[IsActive] = @IsActive,
	[Description] = @Description,
	[Balance] = @Balance,
	[CurrencyCode] = @CurrencyCode,
	[ParentAccountId] = @ParentAccountId,
	[CreatedBy] = @CreatedBy,
	[CreatedAt] = @CreatedAt,
	[UpdatedBy] = @UpdatedBy,
	[UpdatedAt] = @UpdatedAt
	WHERE ( Id = @Id )

	DECLARE @Err int
	DECLARE @Result int
	SET @Result = @@ROWCOUNT
	SET @Err = @@ERROR 

	If @Err <> 0 
	BEGIN
		SET @Result = -1
	END

	RETURN @Result
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[usp_ProductDiscount_Save]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE   PROCEDURE [dbo].[usp_ProductDiscount_Save]

(

    @ProductId       INT,

    @DiscountType    NVARCHAR(50),   -- Flat or Percentage

    @DiscountValue   DECIMAL(18,2),

    @MinQuantity     INT = NULL,

    @EffectiveFrom   DATETIME,

    @EffectiveTo     DATETIME = NULL,

    @CreatedBy       NVARCHAR(100) = NULL

)

AS

BEGIN

    SET NOCOUNT ON;
 
    --------------------------------------------------------

    -- 1. Validate Discount Type

    --------------------------------------------------------

    IF (@DiscountType NOT IN ('Flat', 'Percentage'))

    BEGIN

        RAISERROR('Invalid DiscountType. Only Flat or Percentage allowed.', 16, 1);

        RETURN;

    END
 
    --------------------------------------------------------

    -- 2. Check for existing discount for this product

    --------------------------------------------------------

    DECLARE @ExistingId INT, @ExistingFrom DATETIME, @ExistingTo DATETIME;
 
    SELECT TOP 1 

           @ExistingId = Id,

           @ExistingFrom = EffectiveFrom,

           @ExistingTo = EffectiveTo

    FROM ProductDiscount

    WHERE ProductId = @ProductId

      AND IsActive = 1

    ORDER BY EffectiveFrom DESC;
 
    --------------------------------------------------------

    -- 3. If no previous discount  just insert

    --------------------------------------------------------

    IF (@ExistingId IS NULL)

    BEGIN

        INSERT INTO ProductDiscount

        (

            ProductId, DiscountType, DiscountValue, MinQuantity,

            EffectiveFrom, EffectiveTo, IsActive,

            CreatedBy

        )

        VALUES

        (

            @ProductId, @DiscountType, @DiscountValue, @MinQuantity,

            @EffectiveFrom, @EffectiveTo, 1,

            @CreatedBy

        );

        RETURN;

    END
 
 
    --------------------------------------------------------

    -- 4. If last discount has no end date  auto close it (N2 + C1)

    --------------------------------------------------------

    IF (@ExistingTo IS NULL)

    BEGIN

        UPDATE ProductDiscount

        SET EffectiveTo = DATEADD(DAY, -1, @EffectiveFrom),

            UpdatedAt = SYSDATETIME(),

            UpdatedBy = @CreatedBy

        WHERE Id = @ExistingId;

    END

    ELSE

    BEGIN

        --------------------------------------------------------

        -- 5. Block overlapping date ranges (OD1)

        --------------------------------------------------------

        IF NOT (@EffectiveFrom > @ExistingTo)

        BEGIN

            RAISERROR('Discount period overlaps with existing discount.', 16, 1);

            RETURN;

        END

    END
 
    --------------------------------------------------------

    -- 6. Insert new discount

    --------------------------------------------------------

    INSERT INTO ProductDiscount

    (

        ProductId, DiscountType, DiscountValue, MinQuantity,

        EffectiveFrom, EffectiveTo, IsActive,

        CreatedBy

    )

    VALUES

    (

        @ProductId, @DiscountType, @DiscountValue, @MinQuantity,

        @EffectiveFrom, @EffectiveTo, 1,

        @CreatedBy

    );

END

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[usp_RecordCustomerPaymentJournal]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE   PROCEDURE [dbo].[usp_RecordCustomerPaymentJournal]
    @CustomerPaymentId INT
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    DECLARE @Amount DECIMAL(18,2), @CustomerId INT, @Status NVARCHAR(20);

    SELECT @Amount = Amount, @CustomerId = CustomerId, @Status = Status
    FROM dbo.CustomerPayment
    WHERE Id = @CustomerPaymentId;

    IF @Status <> 'Completed' RETURN;

    DECLARE @JournalId INT;
    INSERT INTO dbo.JournalEntry (ReferenceType, ReferenceId, Description)
    VALUES ('CustomerPayment', @CustomerPaymentId, CONCAT('Customer Payment #', @CustomerPaymentId));

    SET @JournalId = SCOPE_IDENTITY();

    -- Debit Cash
    INSERT INTO dbo.JournalEntryDetail (JournalEntryId, AccountId, Debit)
    SELECT @JournalId, a.Id, @Amount FROM dbo.Account a WHERE a.AccountCode = '1000';

    -- Credit A/R
    INSERT INTO dbo.JournalEntryDetail (JournalEntryId, AccountId, Credit)
    SELECT @JournalId, a.Id, @Amount FROM dbo.Account a WHERE a.AccountCode = '1100';
END;
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[usp_RecordInventory_OUT]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

/***************************************
-- Procedure: usp_RecordInventory_OUT
-- Purpose : Record outbound stock and decrement inventory
-- Rules   : Must supply SalesOrderDetailId (price comes from SalesOrderDetail.UnitPrice unless @SellingPrice provided)
-- Note    : AverageCost is NOT changed on OUT
***************************************/
CREATE   PROCEDURE [dbo].[usp_RecordInventory_OUT]
(
    @ProductId INT,
    @SalesOrderDetailId INT,
    @Quantity INT,
    @SellingPrice DECIMAL(18,2) = NULL  -- optional; if NULL, will use SalesOrderDetail.UnitPrice
)
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    SET XACT_ABORT ON;

    -- basic validation
    IF @SalesOrderDetailId IS NULL
    BEGIN
        RAISERROR('SalesOrderDetailId is required for OUT transactions.',16,1);
        RETURN;
    END

    IF @Quantity <= 0
    BEGIN
        RAISERROR('Quantity must be greater than zero.',16,1);
        RETURN;
    END

    DECLARE @UnitPrice DECIMAL(18,2);

    SELECT @UnitPrice = UnitPrice
    FROM dbo.SalesOrderDetail
    WHERE Id = @SalesOrderDetailId;

    IF @UnitPrice IS NULL
    BEGIN
        RAISERROR('SalesOrderDetail.Id = %d not found or UnitPrice is NULL.',16,1,@SalesOrderDetailId);
        RETURN;
    END

    IF @SellingPrice IS NULL
        SET @SellingPrice = @UnitPrice;

    BEGIN TRANSACTION;
    BEGIN TRY
        DECLARE @CurrentStock INT;

        SELECT @CurrentStock = CurrentStock
        FROM dbo.ProductInventory WITH (UPDLOCK, HOLDLOCK)
        WHERE ProductId = @ProductId;

        IF @CurrentStock IS NULL
        BEGIN
            RAISERROR('No ProductInventory row found for ProductId = %d.',16,1,@ProductId);
            ROLLBACK TRANSACTION;
            RETURN;
        END

        IF @CurrentStock < @Quantity
        BEGIN
            RAISERROR('Insufficient stock for ProductId = %d. Current=%d, Requested=%d',16,1,@ProductId, @CurrentStock, @Quantity);
            ROLLBACK TRANSACTION;
            RETURN;
        END

        -- Insert OUT InventoryTransaction (Price is selling price)
        INSERT INTO dbo.InventoryTransaction (SalesOrderDetailId, ProductId, InOut, Date, Price, Quantity)
        VALUES (@SalesOrderDetailId, @ProductId, N'OUT', SYSUTCDATETIME(), @SellingPrice, @Quantity);

        -- Reduce stock only (AverageCost unchanged)
        UPDATE dbo.ProductInventory
        SET CurrentStock = CurrentStock - @Quantity,
            UpdatedAt = SYSUTCDATETIME()
        WHERE ProductId = @ProductId;

        COMMIT TRANSACTION;
    END TRY
    BEGIN CATCH
        IF XACT_STATE() <> 0
            ROLLBACK TRANSACTION;

        DECLARE @ErrMsg NVARCHAR(4000) = ERROR_MESSAGE();
        RAISERROR('Error in usp_RecordInventory_OUT: %s',16,1,@ErrMsg);
        RETURN;
    END CATCH
END;
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[usp_RecordPurchaseJournal]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE   PROCEDURE [dbo].[usp_RecordPurchaseJournal]
    @PoReceivedId INT
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    DECLARE @Amount DECIMAL(18,2), @VendorId INT;

    SELECT @Amount = BuyingPrice * ReceivedQuantity,
           @VendorId = pr.VendorId
    FROM dbo.PoReceived r
    JOIN dbo.PoRequested pr ON r.PoRequestedId = pr.Id
    WHERE r.Id = @PoReceivedId;

    IF @Amount IS NULL RETURN;

    DECLARE @JournalId INT;
    INSERT INTO dbo.JournalEntry (ReferenceType, ReferenceId, Description)
    VALUES ('PoReceived', @PoReceivedId, CONCAT('Purchase Received #', @PoReceivedId));

    SET @JournalId = SCOPE_IDENTITY();

    -- Debit Inventory
    INSERT INTO dbo.JournalEntryDetail (JournalEntryId, AccountId, Debit)
    SELECT @JournalId, a.Id, @Amount FROM dbo.Account a WHERE a.AccountCode = '1200';

    -- Credit Accounts Payable
    INSERT INTO dbo.JournalEntryDetail (JournalEntryId, AccountId, Credit)
    SELECT @JournalId, a.Id, @Amount FROM dbo.Account a WHERE a.AccountCode = '2000';
END;
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[usp_RecordVendorPaymentJournal]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE   PROCEDURE [dbo].[usp_RecordVendorPaymentJournal]
    @VendorPaymentId INT
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    DECLARE @Amount DECIMAL(18,2), @Status NVARCHAR(20);

    SELECT @Amount = Amount, @Status = Status
    FROM dbo.VendorPayment
    WHERE Id = @VendorPaymentId;

    IF @Status <> 'Completed' RETURN;

    DECLARE @JournalId INT;
    INSERT INTO dbo.JournalEntry (ReferenceType, ReferenceId, Description)
    VALUES ('VendorPayment', @VendorPaymentId, CONCAT('Vendor Payment #', @VendorPaymentId));

    SET @JournalId = SCOPE_IDENTITY();

    -- Debit Accounts Payable
    INSERT INTO dbo.JournalEntryDetail (JournalEntryId, AccountId, Debit)
    SELECT @JournalId, a.Id, @Amount FROM dbo.Account a WHERE a.AccountCode = '2000';

    -- Credit Cash
    INSERT INTO dbo.JournalEntryDetail (JournalEntryId, AccountId, Credit)
    SELECT @JournalId, a.Id, @Amount FROM dbo.Account a WHERE a.AccountCode = '1000';
END;
GO
/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[TR_Account_Audit]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE TRIGGER [dbo].[TR_Account_Audit]
ON [dbo].[Account]
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- INSERT operation
    INSERT INTO [dbo].[AuditLog] (
        TableName,
        Operation,
        PrimaryKeyValue,
        OldValues,
        NewValues,
        ChangedBy,
        ChangeDate
    )
    SELECT
        'Account' AS TableName,
        'INSERT' AS Operation,
        i.Id AS PrimaryKeyValue,
        NULL AS OldValues,
        (
            SELECT i.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER
        ) AS NewValues,
        SUSER_SNAME() AS ChangedBy,
        GETDATE() AS ChangeDate
    FROM inserted i
    WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM deleted d WHERE d.Id = i.Id);

    -- UPDATE operation
    INSERT INTO [dbo].[AuditLog] (
        TableName,
        Operation,
        PrimaryKeyValue,
        OldValues,
        NewValues,
        ChangedBy,
        ChangeDate
    )
    SELECT
        'Account' AS TableName,
        'UPDATE' AS Operation,
        i.Id AS PrimaryKeyValue,
        (
            SELECT d.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER
        ) AS OldValues,
        (
            SELECT i.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER
        ) AS NewValues,
        SUSER_SNAME() AS ChangedBy,
        GETDATE() AS ChangeDate
    FROM inserted i
    INNER JOIN deleted d ON i.Id = d.Id;

    -- DELETE operation
    INSERT INTO [dbo].[AuditLog] (
        TableName,
        Operation,
        PrimaryKeyValue,
        OldValues,
        NewValues,
        ChangedBy,
        ChangeDate
    )
    SELECT
        'Account' AS TableName,
        'DELETE' AS Operation,
        d.Id AS PrimaryKeyValue,
        (
            SELECT d.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER
        ) AS OldValues,
        NULL AS NewValues,
        SUSER_SNAME() AS ChangedBy,
        GETDATE() AS ChangeDate
    FROM deleted d
    WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inserted i WHERE i.Id = d.Id);
END;
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Account] ENABLE TRIGGER [TR_Account_Audit]
GO

/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[trg_Audit_CompanyCustomer]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:53 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

    CREATE TRIGGER [dbo].[trg_Audit_CompanyCustomer]
    ON [dbo].[CompanyCustomer]
    AFTER INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
    AS
    BEGIN
        SET NOCOUNT ON;
        DECLARE @User NVARCHAR(100) = SUSER_SNAME();
        INSERT INTO dbo.AuditLog (TableName, Operation, PrimaryKeyValue, OldValues, NewValues, ChangedBy)
        SELECT
            'CompanyCustomer',
            CASE
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM deleted) AND EXISTS (SELECT * FROM inserted) THEN 'UPDATE'
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM deleted) THEN 'DELETE'
                ELSE 'INSERT'
            END,
            COALESCE(CONVERT(NVARCHAR(100), i.Id), CONVERT(NVARCHAR(100), d.Id)),
            CASE 
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM deleted) THEN 
                    (SELECT * FROM deleted d2 WHERE d2.Id = COALESCE(i.Id, d.Id) FOR JSON AUTO, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER)
                ELSE NULL 
            END,
            CASE 
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM inserted) THEN 
                    (SELECT * FROM inserted i2 WHERE i2.Id = COALESCE(i.Id, d.Id) FOR JSON AUTO, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER)
                ELSE NULL 
            END,
            @User
        FROM inserted i
        FULL JOIN deleted d ON i.Id = d.Id;
    END;
    
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[CompanyCustomer] ENABLE TRIGGER [trg_Audit_CompanyCustomer]
GO

/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[TR_Customer_Audit]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:54 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE TRIGGER [dbo].[TR_Customer_Audit]
ON [dbo].[Customer]
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    DECLARE @Operation NVARCHAR(10);

    -- Handle INSERT
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inserted) AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM deleted)
    BEGIN
        SET @Operation = 'INSERT';

        INSERT INTO [dbo].[AuditLog] (TableName, Operation, PrimaryKeyValue, OldValues, NewValues, ChangedBy, ChangeDate)
        SELECT 
            'Customer',
            @Operation,
            i.Id,
            NULL,
            (SELECT i.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER),
            SUSER_SNAME(),
            GETDATE()
        FROM inserted i;
    END

    -- Handle DELETE
    ELSE IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM deleted) AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inserted)
    BEGIN
        SET @Operation = 'DELETE';

        INSERT INTO [dbo].[AuditLog] (TableName, Operation, PrimaryKeyValue, OldValues, NewValues, ChangedBy, ChangeDate)
        SELECT 
            'Customer',
            @Operation,
            d.Id,
            (SELECT d.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER),
            NULL,
            SUSER_SNAME(),
            GETDATE()
        FROM deleted d;
    END

    -- Handle UPDATE
    ELSE IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inserted) AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM deleted)
    BEGIN
        SET @Operation = 'UPDATE';

        -- Update audit log
        INSERT INTO [dbo].[AuditLog] (TableName, Operation, PrimaryKeyValue, OldValues, NewValues, ChangedBy, ChangeDate)
        SELECT 
            'Customer',
            @Operation,
            i.Id,
            (SELECT d.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER),
            (SELECT i.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER),
            SUSER_SNAME(),
            GETDATE()
        FROM inserted i
        INNER JOIN deleted d ON i.Id = d.Id;

        -- Update UpdatedBy and UpdatedAt in Customer table
        UPDATE c
        SET 
            c.UpdatedBy = SUSER_SNAME(),
            c.UpdatedAt = GETDATE()
        FROM [dbo].[Customer] c
        INNER JOIN inserted i ON c.Id = i.Id;
    END
END;
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Customer] ENABLE TRIGGER [TR_Customer_Audit]
GO

/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[TR_CustomerPayment_Audit]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:54 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE TRIGGER [dbo].[TR_CustomerPayment_Audit]
ON [dbo].[CustomerPayment]
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    DECLARE @Operation NVARCHAR(10);

    -- INSERT
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inserted) AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM deleted)
        SET @Operation = 'INSERT';

    -- DELETE
    ELSE IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM deleted) AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inserted)
        SET @Operation = 'DELETE';

    -- UPDATE
    ELSE
        SET @Operation = 'UPDATE';

    INSERT INTO [dbo].[AuditLog] (
        [TableName],
        [Operation],
        [PrimaryKeyValue],
        [OldValues],
        [NewValues],
        [ChangedBy],
        [ChangeDate]
    )
    SELECT
        'CustomerPayment' AS TableName,
        @Operation AS Operation,
        COALESCE(i.Id, d.Id) AS PrimaryKeyValue,
        CASE 
            WHEN d.Id IS NOT NULL THEN (SELECT d.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER)
            ELSE NULL
        END AS OldValues,
        CASE 
            WHEN i.Id IS NOT NULL THEN (SELECT i.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER)
            ELSE NULL
        END AS NewValues,
        SUSER_SNAME() AS ChangedBy,
        GETDATE() AS ChangeDate
    FROM inserted i
    FULL OUTER JOIN deleted d ON i.Id = d.Id;
END;
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[CustomerPayment] ENABLE TRIGGER [TR_CustomerPayment_Audit]
GO

AFTER INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    DECLARE @Operation NVARCHAR(10);

    -- Identify operation type
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inserted) AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM deleted)
        SET @Operation = 'INSERT';
    ELSE IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM deleted) AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inserted)
        SET @Operation = 'DELETE';
    ELSE
        SET @Operation = 'UPDATE';

    -- Insert into AuditLog
    INSERT INTO [dbo].[AuditLog] (
        [TableName],
        [Operation],
        [PrimaryKeyValue],
        [OldValues],
        [NewValues],
        [ChangedBy],
        [ChangeDate]
    )
    SELECT
        'Delivery' AS TableName,
        @Operation AS Operation,
        COALESCE(i.Id, d.Id) AS PrimaryKeyValue,
        CASE 
            WHEN d.Id IS NOT NULL THEN (SELECT d.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER)
            ELSE NULL
        END AS OldValues,
        CASE 
            WHEN i.Id IS NOT NULL THEN (SELECT i.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER)
            ELSE NULL
        END AS NewValues,
        SUSER_SNAME() AS ChangedBy,
        GETDATE() AS ChangeDate
    FROM inserted i
    FULL OUTER JOIN deleted d ON i.Id = d.Id;
END;

/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[trg_Audit_Language]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:54 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

    CREATE TRIGGER [dbo].[trg_Audit_Language]
    ON [dbo].[Language]
    AFTER INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
    AS
    BEGIN
        SET NOCOUNT ON;
        DECLARE @User NVARCHAR(100) = SUSER_SNAME();
        INSERT INTO dbo.AuditLog (TableName, Operation, PrimaryKeyValue, OldValues, NewValues, ChangedBy)
        SELECT
            'Language',
            CASE
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM deleted) AND EXISTS (SELECT * FROM inserted) THEN 'UPDATE'
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM deleted) THEN 'DELETE'
                ELSE 'INSERT'
            END,
            COALESCE(CONVERT(NVARCHAR(100), i.Id), CONVERT(NVARCHAR(100), d.Id)),
            CASE 
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM deleted) THEN 
                    (SELECT * FROM deleted d2 WHERE d2.Id = COALESCE(i.Id, d.Id) FOR JSON AUTO, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER)
                ELSE NULL 
            END,
            CASE 
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM inserted) THEN 
                    (SELECT * FROM inserted i2 WHERE i2.Id = COALESCE(i.Id, d.Id) FOR JSON AUTO, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER)
                ELSE NULL 
            END,
            @User
        FROM inserted i
        FULL JOIN deleted d ON i.Id = d.Id;
    END;
    
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Language] ENABLE TRIGGER [trg_Audit_Language]
GO

/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[TR_PaymentAllocation_Audit]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:54 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- Trigger for insert/update audit
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[TR_PaymentAllocation_Audit]
ON [dbo].[PaymentAllocation]
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    UPDATE pa
    SET 
        pa.UpdatedAt = SYSDATETIME(),
        pa.UpdatedBy = SUSER_SNAME()
    FROM [dbo].[PaymentAllocation] pa
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON pa.Id = i.Id;

    -- For insert: set CreatedBy/CreatedAt if not already set
    UPDATE pa
    SET 
        pa.CreatedAt = SYSDATETIME(),
        pa.CreatedBy = ISNULL(pa.CreatedBy, SUSER_SNAME())
    FROM [dbo].[PaymentAllocation] pa
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON pa.Id = i.Id
    WHERE pa.CreatedBy IS NULL;
END;
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[PaymentAllocation] ENABLE TRIGGER [TR_PaymentAllocation_Audit]
GO

GO
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[TR_PoReceived_Audit]
ON [dbo].[PoReceived]
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    UPDATE R
    SET 
        R.UpdatedAt = SYSDATETIME(),
        R.UpdatedBy = ISNULL(i.UpdatedBy, SUSER_SNAME())
    FROM [dbo].[PoReceived] R
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON R.Id = i.Id;

    -- Auto fill CreatedBy for new rows
    UPDATE R
    SET 
        R.CreatedBy = ISNULL(R.CreatedBy, SUSER_SNAME())
    FROM [dbo].[PoReceived] R
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON R.Id = i.Id
    LEFT JOIN deleted d ON d.Id = i.Id
    WHERE d.Id IS NULL;
END
GO

CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[TR_PoRequested_Audit]
ON [dbo].[PoRequested]
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    UPDATE R
    SET 
        R.UpdatedAt = SYSDATETIME(),
        R.UpdatedBy = ISNULL(i.UpdatedBy, SUSER_SNAME())
    FROM [dbo].[PoRequested] R
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON R.Id = i.Id;

    -- Set CreatedBy automatically if new
    UPDATE R
    SET 
        R.CreatedBy = ISNULL(R.CreatedBy, SUSER_SNAME())
    FROM [dbo].[PoRequested] R
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON R.Id = i.Id
    LEFT JOIN deleted d ON d.Id = i.Id
    WHERE d.Id IS NULL;  -- new rows only
END
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[PoRequested] ENABLE TRIGGER [TR_PoRequested_Audit]
GO

CREATE TRIGGER [dbo].[trg_Audit_PoRequested]
    ON [dbo].[PoRequested]
    AFTER INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
    AS
    BEGIN
        SET NOCOUNT ON;
        DECLARE @User NVARCHAR(100) = SUSER_SNAME();
        INSERT INTO dbo.AuditLog (TableName, Operation, PrimaryKeyValue, OldValues, NewValues, ChangedBy)
        SELECT
            'PoRequested',
            CASE
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM deleted) AND EXISTS (SELECT * FROM inserted) THEN 'UPDATE'
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM deleted) THEN 'DELETE'
                ELSE 'INSERT'
            END,
            COALESCE(CONVERT(NVARCHAR(100), i.Id), CONVERT(NVARCHAR(100), d.Id)),
            CASE 
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM deleted) THEN 
                    (SELECT * FROM deleted d2 WHERE d2.Id = COALESCE(i.Id, d.Id) FOR JSON AUTO, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER)
                ELSE NULL 
            END,
            CASE 
                WHEN EXISTS (SELECT * FROM inserted) THEN 
                    (SELECT * FROM inserted i2 WHERE i2.Id = COALESCE(i.Id, d.Id) FOR JSON AUTO, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER)
                ELSE NULL 
            END,
            @User
        FROM inserted i
        FULL JOIN deleted d ON i.Id = d.Id;
    END;
GO

/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[TR_SOD_Audit]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:55 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[TR_SOD_Audit]
ON [dbo].[SalesOrderDetail]
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    DECLARE @Operation NVARCHAR(10);
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inserted) AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM deleted)
        SET @Operation = 'INSERT';
    ELSE IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM deleted) AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inserted)
        SET @Operation = 'DELETE';
    ELSE
        SET @Operation = 'UPDATE';

    INSERT INTO [dbo].[AuditLog] (
        TableName, Operation, PrimaryKeyValue, OldValues, NewValues, ChangedBy, ChangeDate
    )
    SELECT
        'SalesOrderDetail',
        @Operation,
        COALESCE(i.Id, d.Id),
        CASE WHEN d.Id IS NOT NULL THEN (SELECT d.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER) END,
        CASE WHEN i.Id IS NOT NULL THEN (SELECT i.* FOR JSON PATH, WITHOUT_ARRAY_WRAPPER) END,
        SUSER_SNAME(),
        GETDATE()
    FROM inserted i
    FULL OUTER JOIN deleted d ON i.Id = d.Id;
END;
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[SalesOrderDetail] ENABLE TRIGGER [TR_SOD_Audit]
GO
/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[TR_SOD_UpdateMetadata]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:55 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[TR_SOD_UpdateMetadata]
ON [dbo].[SalesOrderDetail]
AFTER UPDATE

    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    SET

        s.UpdatedBy = SUSER_SNAME()
    FROM [dbo].[SalesOrderDetail] s
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON s.Id = i.Id;
END;
GO

/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[trg_UpdateProfitAmount]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:55 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE TRIGGER [dbo].[trg_UpdateProfitAmount]
ON [dbo].[SalesOrderDetail]
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    UPDATE sod
    SET ProfitAmount = ROUND((sod.UnitPrice - ISNULL(pi.AverageCost, 0)) * sod.Quantity, 2)
    FROM dbo.SalesOrderDetail sod
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON sod.Id = i.Id
    LEFT JOIN dbo.ProductInventory pi ON pi.ProductId = i.ProductId;
END
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[SalesOrderDetail] ENABLE TRIGGER [trg_UpdateProfitAmount]
GO

/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[trg_SalesOrderHeader_ConfirmUpdate]    Script Date: 11/13/2025 2:10:55 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[trg_SalesOrderHeader_ConfirmUpdate]
ON [dbo].[SalesOrderHeader]
AFTER UPDATE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    UPDATE h
    SET Status = 'Confirmed'
    FROM [dbo].[SalesOrderHeader] h
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON h.Id = i.Id
    WHERE i.SalesChannelId = 1
      AND i.Confirmed = 1
      AND (h.Status <> 'Confirmed' OR h.Status IS NULL);
END;
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[SalesOrderHeader] ENABLE TRIGGER [trg_SalesOrderHeader_ConfirmUpdate]
GO

CREATE   TRIGGER [dbo].[TR_VendorPayment_Audit]
ON [dbo].[VendorPayment]
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    UPDATE vp
    SET 
        vp.UpdatedAt = SYSDATETIME(),
        vp.UpdatedBy = SUSER_SNAME()
    FROM [dbo].[VendorPayment] vp
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON vp.Id = i.Id;

    UPDATE vp
    SET 
        vp.CreatedAt = SYSDATETIME(),
        vp.CreatedBy = ISNULL(vp.CreatedBy, SUSER_SNAME())
    FROM [dbo].[VendorPayment] vp
    INNER JOIN inserted i ON vp.Id = i.Id
    WHERE vp.CreatedBy IS NULL;
END;
GO
